<s> HABAKUK JEPHSON'S STATEMENT XII THAT LITTLE SQUARE BOX THE DEALINGS OF CAPTAIN SHARKEY _and Other Stories of Pirates_ TALES OF PIRATES I CAPTAIN SHARKEY: HOW THE GOVERNOR OF SAINT KITT'S CAME HOME When the great wars of the Spanish Succession had been brought to an end by the Treaty of Utrecht, the vast number of privateers which had been fitted out by the contending parties found their occupation gone </s>
<s> Some took to the more peaceful but less lucrative ways of ordinary commerce, others were absorbed into the fishing-fleets, and a few of the more reckless hoisted the Jolly Rodger at the mizzen and the bloody flag at the main, declaring a private war upon their own account against the whole human race </s>
<s> With mixed crews, recruited from every nation they scoured the seas, disappearing occasionally to careen in some lonely inlet, or putting in for a debauch at some outlaying port, where they dazzled the inhabitants by their lavishness and horrified them by their brutalities </s>
<s> On the Coromandel Coast, at Madagascar, in the African waters, and above all in the West Indian and American seas, the pirates were a constant menace </s>
<s> With an insolent luxury they would regulate their depredations by the comfort of the seasons, harrying New England in the summer and dropping south again to the tropical islands in the winter </s>
<s> They were the more to be dreaded because they had none of that discipline and restraint which made their predecessors, the Buccaneers, both formidable and respectable </s>
<s> These Ishmaels of the sea rendered an account to no man, and treated their prisoners according to the drunken whim of the moment </s>
<s> Flashes of grotesque generosity alternated with longer stretches of inconceivable ferocity, and the skipper who fell into their hands might find himself dismissed with his cargo, after serving as boon companion in some hideous debauch, or might sit at his cabin table with his own nose and his lips served up with pepper and salt in front of him </s>
<s> It took a stout seaman in those days to ply his calling in the Caribbean Gulf </s>
<s> Such a man was Captain John Scarrow, of the ship _Morning Star_, and yet he breathed a long sigh of relief when he heard the splash of the falling anchor and swung at his moorings within a hundred yards of the guns of the citadel of Basseterre </s>
<s> St </s>
<s> Kitt's was his final port of call, and early next morning his bowsprit would be pointed for Old England </s>
<s> He had had enough of those robber-haunted seas </s>
<s> Ever since he had left Maracaibo upon the Main, with his full lading of sugar and red pepper, he had winced at every topsail which glimmered over the violet edge of the tropical sea </s>
<s> He had coasted up the Windward Islands, touching here and there, and assailed continually by stories of villainy and outrage </s>
<s> Captain Sharkey, of the 20-gun pirate barque, _Happy Delivery_, had passed down the coast, and had littered it with gutted vessels and with murdered men </s>
<s> Dreadful anecdotes were current of his grim pleasantries and of his inflexible ferocity </s>
<s> From the Bahamas to the Main his coal-black barque, with the ambiguous name, had been freighted with death and many things which are worse than death </s>
<s> So nervous was Captain Scarrow, with his new full-rigged ship and her full and valuable lading, that he struck out to the west as far as Bird's Island to be out of the usual track of commerce </s>
<s> And yet even in those solitary waters he had been unable to shake off sinister traces of Captain Sharkey </s>
<s> One morning they had raised a single skiff adrift upon the face of the ocean </s>
<s> Its only occupant was a delirious seaman, who yelled hoarsely as they hoisted him aboard, and showed a dried-up tongue like a black and wrinkled fungus at the back of his mouth </s>
<s> Water and nursing soon transformed him into the strongest and smartest sailor on the ship </s>
<s> He was from Marblehead, in New England, it seemed, and was the sole survivor of a schooner which had been scuttled by the dreadful Sharkey </s>
<s> For a week Hiram Evanson, for that was his name, had been adrift beneath a tropical sun </s>
<s> Sharkey had ordered the mangled remains of his late captain to be thrown into the boat, "as provisions for the voyage," but the seaman had at once committed them to the deep, lest the temptation should be more than he could bear </s>
<s> He had lived upon his own huge frame, until, at the last moment, the _Morning Star_ had found him in that madness which is the precursor of such a death </s>
<s> It was no bad find for Captain Scarrow, for, with a short-handed crew, such a seaman as this big New Englander was a prize worth having </s>
<s> He vowed that he was the only man whom Captain Sharkey had ever placed under an obligation </s>
<s> Now that they lay under the guns of Basseterre, all danger from the pirate was at an end, and yet the thought of him lay heavily upon the seaman's mind as he watched the agent's boat shooting out from the custom-house quay </s>
<s> "I'll lay you a wager, Morgan," said he to the first mate, "that the agent will speak of Sharkey in the first hundred words that pass his lips" </s>
<s> "Well, captain, I'll have you a silver dollar, and chance it," said the rough old Bristol man beside him </s>
<s> The negro rowers shot the boat alongside, and the linen-clad steersman sprang up the ladder </s>
<s> "Welcome, Captain Scarrow" </s>
<s> he cried </s>
<s> "Have you heard about Sharkey" </s>
<s> The captain grinned at the mate </s>
<s> "What devilry has he been up to now" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> "Devilry </s>
<s> You've not heard, then </s>
<s> Why, we've got him safe under lock and key here at Basseterre </s>
<s> He was tried last Wednesday, and he is to be hanged to-morrow morning" </s>
<s> Captain and mate gave a shout of joy, which an instant later was taken up by the crew </s>
<s> Discipline was forgotten as they scrambled up through the break of the poop to hear the news </s>
<s> The New Englander was in the front of them with a radiant face turned up to heaven, for he came of the Puritan stock </s>
<s> "Sharkey to be hanged" </s>
<s> he cried </s>

<s> cried the mate, whose outraged sense of discipline was even stronger than his interest at the news </s>
<s> "I'll pay that dollar, Captain Scarrow, with the lightest heart that ever I paid a wager yet </s>
<s> How came the villain to be taken" </s>
<s> "Why, as to that, he became more than his own comrades could abide, and they took such a horror of him that they would not have him on the ship </s>
<s> So they marooned him upon the Little Mangles to the south of the Mysteriosa Bank, and there he was found by a Portobello trader, who brought him in </s>
<s> There was talk of sending him to Jamaica to be tried, but our good little governor, Sir Charles Ewan, would not hear of it </s>
<s> 'He's my meat,' said he, 'and I claim the cooking of it' </s>
<s> If you can stay till to-morrow morning at ten, you'll see the joint swinging" </s>
<s> "I wish I could," said the captain, wistfully, "but I am sadly behind time now </s>
<s> I should start with the evening tide" </s>
<s> "That you can't do," said the agent with decision </s>
<s> "The Governor is going back with you" </s>
<s> "The Governor" </s>
<s> "Yes </s>
<s> He's had a dispatch from Government to return without delay </s>
<s> The fly-boat that brought it has gone on to Virginia </s>
<s> So Sir Charles has been waiting for you, as I told him you were due before the rains" </s>
<s> "Well, well" </s>
<s> cried the captain, in some perplexity, "I'm a plain seaman, and I don't know much of governors and baronets and their ways </s>
<s> I don't remember that I ever so much as spoke to one </s>
<s> But if it's in King George's service, and he asks a cast in the _Morning Star_ as far as London, I'll do what I can for him </s>
<s> There's my own cabin he can have and welcome </s>
<s> As to the cooking, it's lobscouse and salmagundy six days in the week; but he can bring his own cook aboard with him if he thinks our galley too rough for his taste" </s>
<s> "You need not trouble your mind, Captain Scarrow," said the agent </s>
<s> "Sir Charles is in weak health just now, only clear of a quartan ague, and it is likely he will keep his cabin most of the voyage </s>
<s> Dr </s>
<s> Larousse said that he would have sunk had the hanging of Sharkey not put fresh life into him </s>
<s> He has a great spirit in him, though, and you must not blame him if he is somewhat short in his speech" </s>
<s> "He may say what he likes and do what he likes so long as he does not come athwart my hawse when I am working the ship," said the captain </s>
<s> "He is Governor of St </s>
<s> Kitt's, but I am Governor of the _Morning Star_ </s>
<s> And, by his leave, I must weigh with the first tide, for I owe a duty to my employer, just as he does to King George" </s>
<s> "He can scarce be ready to-night, for he has many things to set in order before he leaves" </s>
<s> "The early morning tide, then" </s>
<s> "Very good </s>
<s> I shall send his things aboard to-night, and he will follow them to-morrow early if I can prevail upon him to leave St </s>
<s> Kitt's without seeing Sharkey do the rogue's hornpipe </s>
<s> His own orders were instant, so it may be that he will come at once </s>
<s> It is likely that Dr </s>
<s> Larousse may attend him upon the journey" </s>
<s> Left to themselves, the captain and mate made the best preparations which they could for their illustrious passenger </s>
<s> The largest cabin was turned out and adorned in his honour, and orders were given by which barrels of fruit and some cases of wine should be brought off to vary the plain food of an ocean-going trader </s>
<s> In the evening the Governor's baggage began to arrive--great ironbound ant-proof trunks, and official tin packing-cases, with other strange-shaped packages, which suggested the cocked hat or the sword within </s>
<s> And then there came a note, with a heraldic device upon the big red seal, to say that Sir Charles Ewan made his compliments to Captain Scarrow, and that he hoped to be with him in the morning as early as his duties and his infirmities would permit </s>
<s> He was as good as his word, for the first grey of dawn had hardly begun to deepen into pink when he was brought alongside, and climbed with some difficulty up the ladder </s>
<s> The captain had heard that the Governor was an eccentric, but he was hardly prepared for the curious figure who came limping feebly down his quarter-deck, his steps supported by a thick bamboo cane </s>
<s> He wore a Ramillies wig, all twisted into little tails like a poodle's coat, and cut so low across the brow that the large green glasses which covered his eyes looked as if they were hung from it </s>
<s> A fierce beak of a nose, very long and very thin, cut the air in front of him </s>
<s> His ague had caused him to swathe his throat and chin with a broad linen cravat, and he wore a loose damask powdering-gown secured by a cord round the waist </s>
<s> As he advanced he carried his masterful nose high in the air, but his head turned slowly from side to side in the helpless manner of the purblind, and he called in a high, querulous voice for the captain </s>
<s> "You have my things" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> "Yes, Sir Charles" </s>
<s> "Have you wine aboard" </s>
<s> "I have ordered five cases, sir" </s>
<s> "And tobacco" </s>
<s> "There is a keg of Trinidad" </s>
<s> "You play a hand at piquet" </s>
<s> "Passably well, sir" </s>
<s> "Then up anchor, and to sea" </s>
<s> There was a fresh westerly wind, so by the time the sun was fairly through the morning haze, the ship was hull down from the islands </s>
<s> The decrepit Governor still limped the deck, with one guiding hand upon the quarter-rail </s>
<s> "You are on Government service now, Captain," said he </s>
<s> "They are counting the days till I come to Westminster, I promise you </s>

<s> "Every inch, Sir Charles" </s>
<s> "Keep her so if you blow the sails out of her </s>

<s> "I am honoured in enjoying your Excellency's society," said the Captain </s>
<s> "But I am sorry that your eyes should be so afflicted" </s>
<s> "Yes, indeed </s>

<s> "Yes; I have had a pyrexy, which has reduced me much" </s>

<s> "Ah, the rascal </s>
<s> There was no budging him, for he has a snug business amongst the merchants </s>

<s> "There's an end of Sharkey" </s>
<s> cried the captain; and the crew took up the cry as they gathered in little knots upon the deck and stared back at the low, purple line of the vanishing land </s>
<s> It was a cheering omen for their start across the Western Ocean, and the invalid Governor found himself a popular man on board, for it was generally understood that but for his insistence upon an immediate trial and sentence, the villain might have played upon some more venal judge and so escaped </s>
<s> At dinner that day Sir Charles gave many anecdotes of the deceased pirate; and so affable was he, and so skilful in adapting his conversation to men of lower degree, that captain, mate, and Governor smoked their long pipes and drank their claret as three good comrades should </s>
<s> "And what figure did Sharkey cut in the dock" </s>
<s> asked the captain </s>
<s> "He is a man of some presence," said the Governor </s>
<s> "I had always understood that he was an ugly, sneering devil," remarked the mate </s>
<s> "Well, I dare say he could look ugly upon occasions," said the Governor </s>
<s> "I have heard a New Bedford whaleman say that he could not forget his eyes," said Captain Scarrow </s>
<s> "They were of the lightest filmy blue, with red-rimmed lids </s>
<s> Was that not so, Sir Charles" </s>
<s> "Alas, my own eyes will not permit me to know much of those of others </s>
<s> But I remember now that the Adjutant-General said that he had such an eye as you describe, and added that the jury were so foolish as to be visibly discomposed when it was turned upon them </s>
<s> It is well for them that he is dead, for he was a man who would never forget an injury, and if he had laid hands upon any one of them he would have stuffed him with straw and hung him for a figure-head" </s>
<s> The idea seemed to amuse the Governor, for he broke suddenly into a high, neighing laugh, and the two seamen laughed also, but not so heartily, for they remembered that Sharkey was not the last pirate who sailed the western seas, and that as grotesque a fate might come to be their own </s>
<s> Another bottle was broached to drink to a pleasant voyage, and the Governor would drink just one other on the top of it, so that the seamen were glad at last to stagger off--the one to his watch and the other to his bunk </s>
<s> But when after his four hours' spell the mate came down again, he was amazed to see the Governor in his Ramillies wig, his glasses, and his powdering-gown still seated sedately at the lonely table with his reeking pipe and six black bottles by his side </s>
<s> "I have drunk with the Governor of St </s>
<s> Kitt's when he was sick," said he, "and God forbid that I should ever try to keep pace with him when he is well" </s>
<s> The voyage of the _Morning Star_ was a successful one, and in about three weeks she was at the mouth of the British Channel </s>
<s> From the first day the infirm Governor had begun to recover his strength, and before they were half-way across the Atlantic he was, save only for his eyes, as well as any man upon the ship </s>
<s> Those who uphold the nourishing qualities of wine might point to him in triumph, for never a night passed that he did not repeat the performance of his first one </s>
<s> And yet he would be out upon deck in the early morning as fresh and brisk as the best of them, peering about with his weak eyes, and asking questions about the sails and the rigging, for he was anxious to learn the ways of the sea </s>
<s> And he made up for the deficiency of his eyes by obtaining leave from the captain that the New England seaman--he who had been cast away in the boat--should lead him about, and above all that he should sit beside him when he played cards and count the number of the pips, for unaided he could not tell the king from the knave </s>
<s> It was natural that this Evanson should do the Governor willing service, since the one was the victim of the vile Sharkey, and the other was his avenger </s>
<s> One could see that it was a pleasure to the big American to lend his arm to the invalid, and at night he would stand with all respect behind his chair in the cabin and lay his great stub-nailed forefinger upon the card which he should play </s>
<s> Between them there was little in the pockets either of Captain Scarrow or of Morgan, the first mate, by the time they sighted the Lizard </s>
<s> And it was not long before they found that all they had heard of the high temper of Sir Charles Ewan fell short of the mark </s>
<s> At a sign of opposition or a word of argument his chin would shoot out from his cravat, his masterful nose would be cocked at a higher and more insolent angle, and his bamboo cane would whistle up over his shoulder </s>
<s> He cracked it once over the head of the carpenter when the man had accidentally jostled him upon the deck </s>
<s> Once, too, when there was some grumbling and talk of a mutiny over the state of the provisions, he was of opinion that they should not wait for the dogs to rise, but that they should march forward and set upon them until they had trounced the devilment out of them </s>

<s> Kitt's, killing became murder upon the high seas </s>

<s> II THE DEALINGS OF CAPTAIN SHARKEY WITH STEPHEN CRADDOCK Careening was a very necessary operation for the old pirate </s>
<s> On his superior speed he depended both for overhauling the trader and escaping the man-of-war </s>
<s> But it was impossible to retain his sailing qualities unless he periodically--once a year, at the least--cleared his vessel's bottom from the long, trailing plants and crusting barnacles which gather so rapidly in the tropical seas </s>
<s> For this purpose he lightened his vessel, thrust her into some narrow inlet where she would be left high and dry at low water, fastened blocks and tackles to her masts to pull her over on to her bilge, and then scraped her thoroughly from rudder-post to cutwater </s>
<s> During the weeks which were thus occupied the ship was, of course, defenceless; but, on the other hand, she was unapproachable by anything heavier than an empty hull, and the place for careening was chosen with an eye to secrecy, so that there was no great danger </s>
<s> So secure did the captains feel, that it was not uncommon for them, at such times, to leave their ships under a sufficient guard and to start off in the long-boat, either upon a sporting expedition or, more frequently, upon a visit to some outlying town, where they turned the heads of the women by their swaggering gallantry, or broached pipes of wine in the market square, with a threat to pistol all who would not drink with them </s>
<s> Sometimes they would even appear in cities of the size of Charleston, and walk the streets with their clattering sidearms--an open scandal to the whole law-abiding colony </s>
<s> Such visits were not always paid with impunity </s>
<s> It was one of them, for example, which provoked Lieutenant Maynard to hack off Blackbeard's head, and to spear it upon the end of his bowsprit </s>
<s> But, as a rule, the pirate ruffled and bullied and drabbed without let or hindrance, until it was time for him to go back to his ship once more </s>
<s> There was one pirate, however, who never crossed even the skirts of civilisation, and that was the sinister Sharkey, of the barque _Happy Delivery_ </s>
<s> It may have been from his morose and solitary temper, or, as is more probable, that he knew that his name upon the coast was such that outraged humanity would, against all odds, have thrown themselves upon him, but never once did he show his face in a settlement </s>
<s> When his ship was laid up he would leave her under the charge of Ned Galloway--her New England quartermaster--and would take long voyages in his boat, sometimes, it was said, for the purpose of burying his share of the plunder, and sometimes to shoot the wild oxen of Hispaniola, which, when dressed and barbecued, provided provisions for his next voyage </s>
<s> In the latter case the barque would come round to some pre-arranged spot to pick him up and take on board what he had shot </s>
<s> There had always been a hope in the islands that Sharkey might be taken on one of these occasions; and at last there came news to Kingston which seemed to justify an attempt upon him </s>
<s> It was brought by an elderly logwood-cutter who had fallen into the pirate's hands, and in some freak of drunken benevolence had been allowed to get away with nothing worse than a slit nose and a drubbing </s>
<s> His account was recent and definite </s>
<s> The _Happy Delivery_ was careening at Torbec on the south-west of Hispaniola </s>
<s> Sharkey, with four men, was buccaneering on the outlying island of La Vache </s>
<s> The blood of a hundred murdered crews was calling out for vengeance, and now at last it seemed as if it might not call in vain </s>
<s> Sir Edward Compton, the high-nosed, red-faced Governor, sitting in solemn conclave with the commandant and the head of the council, was sorely puzzled in his mind as to how he should use his chance </s>
<s> There was no man-of-war nearer than Jamestown, and she was a clumsy old fly-boat, which could neither overhaul the pirate on the seas, nor reach her in a shallow inlet </s>
<s> There were forts and artillerymen both at Kingston and Port Royal, but no soldiers available for an expedition </s>
<s> A private venture might be fitted out--and there were many who had a blood-feud with Sharkey--but what could a private venture do </s>
<s> The pirates were numerous and desperate </s>
<s> As to taking Sharkey and his four companions, that, of course, would be easy if they could get at them; but how were they to get at them on a large well-wooded island like La Vache, full of wild hills and impenetrable jungles </s>
<s> A reward was offered to whoever could find a solution, and that brought a man to the front who had a singular plan, and was himself prepared to carry it out </s>
<s> Stephen Craddock had been that most formidable person, the Puritan gone wrong </s>
<s> Sprung from a decent Salem family, his ill-doing seemed to be a recoil from the austerity of their religion, and he brought to vice all the physical strength and energy with which the virtues of his ancestors had endowed him </s>
<s> He was ingenious, fearless, and exceedingly tenacious of purpose, so that when he was still young his name became notorious upon the American coast </s>

<s> III THE BLIGHTING OF SHARKEY Sharkey, the abominable Sharkey, was out again </s>
<s> After two years of the Coromandel coast, his black barque of death, the _Happy Delivery_, was prowling off the Spanish Main, while trader and fisher flew for dear life at the menace of that patched fore-topsail, rising slowly over the violet rim of the tropical sea </s>
<s> As the birds cower when the shadow of the hawk falls athwart the field, or as the jungle folk crouch and shiver when the coughing cry of the tiger is heard in the night-time, so through all the busy world of ships, from the whalers of Nantucket to the tobacco ships of Charleston, and from the Spanish supply ships of Cadiz to the sugar merchants of the Main, there spread the rumour of the black curse of the ocean </s>
<s> Some hugged the shore, ready to make for the nearest port, while others struck far out beyond the known lines of commerce, but none were so stout-hearted that they did not breathe more freely when their passengers and cargoes were safe under the guns of some mothering fort </s>
<s> Through all the islands there ran tales of charred derelicts at sea, of sudden glares seen afar in the night-time, and of withered bodies stretched upon the sand of waterless Bahama Keys </s>
<s> All the old signs were there to show that Sharkey was at his bloody game once more </s>
<s> These fair waters and yellow-rimmed palm-nodding islands are the traditional home of the sea rover </s>
<s> First it was the gentleman adventurer, the man of family and honour, who fought as a patriot, though he was ready to take his payment in Spanish plunder </s>
<s> Then, within a century, his debonair figure had passed to make room for the buccaneers, robbers pure and simple, yet with some organised code of their own, commanded by notable chieftains, and taking in hand great concerted enterprises </s>
<s> They, too, passed with their fleets and their sacking of cities, to make room for the worst of all, the lonely, outcast pirate, the bloody Ishmael of the seas, at war with the whole human race </s>
<s> This was the vile brood which the early eighteenth century had spawned forth, and of them all there was none who could compare in audacity, wickedness, and evil repute with the unutterable Sharkey </s>
<s> It was early in May, in the year 1720, that the _Happy Delivery_ lay with her fore-yard aback some five leagues west of the Windward Passage, waiting to see what rich, helpless craft the trade-wind might bring down to her </s>
<s> Three days she had lain there, a sinister black speck, in the centre of the great sapphire circle of the ocean </s>
<s> Far to the south-east the low blue hills of Hispaniola showed up on the skyline </s>
<s> Hour by hour as he waited without avail, Sharkey's savage temper had risen, for his arrogant spirit chafed against any contradiction, even from Fate itself </s>
<s> To his quartermaster, Ned Galloway, he had said that night, with his odious neighing laugh, that the crew of the next captured vessel should answer to him for having kept him waiting so long </s>
<s> The cabin of the pirate barque was a good-sized room, hung with much tarnished finery, and presenting a strange medley of luxury and disorder </s>
<s> The panelling of carved and polished sandal-wood was blotched with foul smudges and chipped with bullet-marks fired in some drunken revelry </s>

<s> * * * * * Extract from the log of H.M </s>
<s> fifty-gun ship _Hecate_ in her cruise off the American Main </s>
<s> "_Jan </s>
<s> 26, 1721._--This day, the junk having become unfit for food, and five of the crew down with scurvy, I ordered that we send two boats ashore at the nor'-western point of Hispaniola, to seek for fresh fruit, and perchance shoot some of the wild oxen with which the island abounds </s>
<s> "_7 p.m._--The boats have returned with good store of green stuff and two bullocks </s>
<s> Mr Woodruff, the master, reports that near the landing-place at the edge of the forest was found the skeleton of a woman, clad in European dress, of such sort as to show that she may have been a person of quality </s>
<s> Her head had been crushed by a great stone which lay beside her </s>
<s> Hard by was a grass hut, and signs that a man had dwelt therein for some time, as was shown by charred wood, bones and other traces </s>
<s> There is a rumour upon the coast that Sharkey, the bloody pirate, was marooned in these parts last year, but whether he has made his way into the interior, or whether he has been picked up by some craft, there is no means of knowing </s>
<s> If he be once again afloat, then I pray that God send him under our guns" </s>
<s> IV HOW COPLEY BANKS SLEW CAPTAIN SHARKEY The Buccaneers were something higher than a mere band of marauders </s>
<s> They were a floating republic, with laws, usages, and discipline of their own </s>
<s> In their endless and remorseless quarrel with the Spaniards they had some semblance of right upon their side </s>
<s> Their bloody harryings of the cities of the Main were not more barbarous than the inroads of Spain upon the Netherlands--or upon the Caribs in these same American lands </s>
<s> The chief of the Buccaneers, were he English or French, a Morgan or a Granmont, was still a responsible person, whose country might countenance him, or even praise him, so long as he refrained from any deed which might shock the leathery seventeenth-century conscience too outrageously </s>
<s> Some of them were touched with religion, and it is still remembered how Sawkins threw the dice overboard upon the Sabbath, and Daniel pistolled a man before the altar for irreverence </s>
<s> But there came a day when the fleets of the Buccaneers no longer mustered at the Tortugas, and the solitary and outlawed pirate took their place </s>
<s> Yet even with him the tradition of restraint and of discipline still lingered; and among the early pirates, the Avorys, the Englands, and the Robertses, there remained some respect for human sentiment </s>
<s> They were more dangerous to the merchant than to the seaman </s>
<s> But they in turn were replaced by more savage and desperate men, who frankly recognised that they would get no quarter in their war with the human race, and who swore that they would give as little as they got </s>
<s> Of their histories we know little that is trustworthy </s>
<s> They wrote no memoirs and left no trace, save an occasional blackened and blood-stained derelict adrift upon the face of the Atlantic </s>
<s> Their deeds could only be surmised from the long roll of ships which never made their port </s>
<s> Searching the records of history, it is only here and there in an old-world trial that the veil that shrouds them seems for an instant to be lifted, and we catch a glimpse of some amazing and grotesque brutality behind </s>
<s> Such was the breed of Ned Low, of Gow the Scotchman, and of the infamous Sharkey, whose coal-black barque, the _Happy Delivery_, was known from the Newfoundland Banks to the mouths of the Orinoco as the dark forerunner of misery and of death </s>
<s> There were many men, both among the islands and on the main, who had a blood feud with Sharkey, but not one who had suffered more bitterly than Copley Banks, of Kingston </s>
<s> Banks had been one of the leading sugar merchants of the West Indies </s>
<s> He was a man of position, a member of the Council, the husband of a Percival, and the cousin of the Governor of Virginia </s>
<s> His two sons had been sent to London to be educated, and their mother had gone over to bring them back </s>
<s> On their return voyage the ship, the _Duchess of Cornwall_, fell into the hands of Sharkey, and the whole family met with an infamous death </s>
<s> Copley Banks said little when he heard the news, but he sank into a morose and enduring melancholy </s>
<s> He neglected his business, avoided his friends, and spent much of his time in the low taverns of the fishermen and seamen </s>
<s> There, amidst riot and devilry, he sat silently puffing at his pipe, with a set face and a smouldering eye </s>
<s> It was generally supposed that his misfortunes had shaken his wits, and his old friends looked at him askance, for the company which he kept was enough to bar him from honest men </s>
<s> From time to time there came rumours of Sharkey over the sea </s>
<s> Sometimes it was from some schooner which had seen a great flame upon the horizon, and approaching to offer help to the burning ship, had fled away at the sight of the sleek, black barque, lurking like a wolf near a mangled sheep </s>
<s> Sometimes it was a frightened trader, which had come tearing in with her canvas curved like a lady's bodice, because she had seen a patched fore-topsail rising slowly above the violet water-line </s>
<s> Sometimes it was from a Coaster, which had found a waterless Bahama Cay littered with sun-dried bodies </s>
<s> Once there came a man who had been mate of a Guineaman, and who had escaped from the pirate's hands </s>
<s> He could not speak--for reasons which Sharkey could best supply--but he could write, and he did write, to the very great interest of Copley Banks </s>
<s> For hours they sat together over the map, and the dumb man pointed here and there to outlying reefs and tortuous inlets, while his companion sat smoking in silence, with his unvarying face and his fiery eyes </s>
<s> One morning, some two years after his misfortune, Mr Copley Banks strode into his own office with his old air of energy and alertness </s>
<s> The manager stared at him in surprise, for it was months since he had shown any interest in business </s>
<s> "Good morning, Mr Banks" </s>
<s> said he </s>
<s> "Good morning, Freeman </s>
<s> I see that _Ruffling Harry_ is in the Bay" </s>
<s> "Yes, sir; she clears for the Windward Islands on Wednesday" </s>
<s> "I have other plans for her, Freeman </s>
<s> I have determined upon a slaving venture to Whydah" </s>
<s> "But her cargo is ready, sir" </s>
<s> "Then it must come out again, Freeman </s>
<s> My mind is made up, and the _Ruffling Harry_ must go slaving to Whydah" </s>
<s> All argument and persuasion were vain, so the manager had dolefully to clear the ship once more </s>
<s> And then Copley Banks began to make preparations for his African voyage </s>
<s> It appeared that he relied upon force rather than barter for the filling of his hold, for he carried none of those showy trinkets which savages love, but the brig was fitted with eight nine-pounder guns and racks full of muskets and cutlasses </s>
<s> The after sail-room next the cabin was transformed into a powder magazine, and she carried as many round shot as a well-found privateer </s>
<s> Water and provisions were shipped for a long voyage </s>
<s> But the preparation of his ship's company was most surprising </s>
<s> It made Freeman, the manager, realise that there was truth in the rumour that his master had taken leave of his senses </s>
<s> For, under one pretext or another, he began to dismiss the old and tried hands, who had served the firm for years, and in their place he embarked the scum of the port--men whose reputations were so vile that the lowest crimp would have been ashamed to furnish them </s>
<s> There was Birthmark Sweetlocks, who was known to have been present at the killing of the log-wood cutters, so that his hideous scarlet disfigurement was put down by the fanciful as being a red afterglow from that great crime </s>
<s> He was first mate, and under him was Israel Martin, a little sun-wilted fellow who had served with Howell Davies at the taking of Cape Coast Castle </s>
<s> The crew were chosen from amongst those whom Banks had met and known in their own infamous haunts, and his own table-steward was a haggard-faced man, who gobbled at you when he tried to talk </s>
<s> His beard had been shaved, and it was impossible to recognise him as the same man whom Sharkey had placed under the knife, and who had escaped to tell his experiences to Copley Banks </s>
<s> These doings were not unnoticed, nor yet uncommented upon in the town of Kingston </s>
<s> The Commandant of the troops--Major Harvey, of the Artillery--made serious representations to the Governor </s>
<s> "She is not a trader, but a small warship," said he </s>
<s> "I think it would be as well to arrest Copley Banks and to seize the vessel" </s>
<s> "What do you suspect" </s>
<s> asked the Governor, who was a slow-witted man, broken down with fevers and port wine </s>
<s> "I suspect," said the soldier, "that it is Stede Bonnet over again" </s>
<s> Now, Stede Bonnet was a planter of high reputation and religious character, who, from some sudden and overpowering freshet of wildness in his blood, had given up everything in order to start off pirating in the Caribbean Sea </s>
<s> The example was a recent one, and it had caused the utmost consternation in the islands </s>
<s> Governors had before now been accused of being in league with pirates, and of receiving commissions upon their plunder, so that any want of vigilance was open to a sinister construction </s>
<s> "Well, Major Harvey," said he, "I am vastly sorry to do anything which may offend my friend Copley Banks, for many a time have my knees been under his mahogany, but in face of what you say there is no choice for me but to order you to board the vessel and to satisfy yourself as to her character and destination" </s>
<s> So at one in the morning Major Harvey, with a launchful of his soldiers, paid a surprise visit to the _Ruffling Harry_, with the result that they picked up nothing more solid than a hempen cable floating at the moorings </s>
<s> It had been slipped by the brig, whose owner had scented danger </s>
<s> She had already passed the Palisades, and was beating out against the north-east trades on a course for the Windward Passage </s>
<s> When upon the next morning the brig had left Morant Point a mere haze upon the Southern horizon, the men were called aft, and Copley Banks revealed his plans to them </s>
<s> He had chosen them, he said, as brisk boys and lads of spirit, who would rather run some risk upon the sea than starve for a living upon the shore </s>
<s> King's ships were few and weak, and they could master any trader who might come their way </s>
<s> Others had done well at the business, and with a handy, well-found vessel, there was no reason why they should not turn their tarry jackets into velvet coats </s>
<s> If they were prepared to sail under the black flag, he was ready to command them; but if any wished to withdraw, they might have the gig and row back to Jamaica </s>
<s> Four men out of six-and-forty asked for their discharge, went over the ship's side into the boat, and rowed away amidst the jeers and howlings of the crew </s>
<s> The rest assembled aft, and drew up the articles of their association </s>
<s> A square of black tarpaulin had the white skull painted upon it, and was hoisted amidst cheering at the main </s>
<s> Officers were elected, and the limits of their authority fixed </s>
<s> Copley Banks was chosen Captain, but, as there are no mates upon a pirate craft, Birthmark Sweetlocks became quartermaster, and Israel Martin the boatswain </s>
<s> There was no difficulty in knowing what was the custom of the brotherhood, for half the men at least had served upon pirates before </s>
<s> Food should be the same for all, and no man should interfere with another man's drink </s>
<s> The Captain should have a cabin, but all hands should be welcome to enter it when they chose </s>
<s> All should share and share alike, save only the captain, quartermaster, boatswain, carpenter, and master-gunner, who had from a quarter to a whole share extra </s>
<s> He who saw a prize first should have the best weapon taken out of her </s>
<s> He who boarded her first should have the richest suit of clothes aboard of her </s>
<s> Every man might treat his own prisoner, be it man or woman, after his own fashion </s>
<s> If a man flinched from his gun, the quartermaster should pistol him </s>
<s> These were some of the rules which the crew of the _Ruffling Harry_ subscribed by putting forty-two crosses at the foot of the paper upon which they had been drawn </s>
<s> So a new rover was afloat upon the seas, and her name before a year was over became as well known as that of the _Happy Delivery_ </s>
<s> From the Bahamas to the Leewards, and from the Leewards to the Windwards, Copley Banks became the rival of Sharkey and the terror of traders </s>
<s> For a long time the barque and the brig never met, which was the more singular, as the _Ruffling Harry_ was for ever looking in at Sharkey's resorts; but at last one day, when she was passing down the inlet of Coxon's Hole, at the east end of Cuba, with the intention of careening, there was the _Happy Delivery_, with her blocks and tackle-falls already rigged for the same purpose </s>
<s> Copley Banks fired a shotted salute and hoisted the green trumpeter ensign, as the custom was among gentlemen of the sea </s>
<s> Then he dropped his boat and went aboard </s>
<s> Captain Sharkey was not a man of a genial mood, nor had he any kindly sympathy for those who were of the same trade as himself </s>
<s> Copley Banks found him seated astride upon one of the after guns, with his New England quartermaster, Ned Galloway, and a crowd of roaring ruffians standing about him </s>
<s> Yet none of them roared with quite such assurance when Sharkey's pale face and filmy blue eyes were turned upon him </s>
<s> He was in his shirt-sleeves, with his cambric frills breaking through his open red satin long-flapped vest </s>
<s> The scorching sun seemed to have no power upon his fleshless frame, for he wore a low fur cap, as though it had been winter </s>
<s> A many-coloured band of silk passed across his body and supported a short murderous sword, while his broad, brass-buckled belt was stuffed with pistols </s>
<s> "Sink you for a poacher" </s>
<s> he cried, as Copley Banks passed over the bulwarks </s>
<s> "I will drub you within an inch of your life, and that inch also </s>
<s> What mean you by fishing in my waters" </s>
<s> Copley Banks looked at him, and his eyes were like those of a traveller who sees his home at last </s>
<s> "I am glad that we are of one mind," said he, "for I am myself of opinion that the seas are not large enough for the two of us </s>
<s> But if you will take your sword and pistols and come upon a sand-bank with me, then the world will be rid of a damned villain whichever way it goes" </s>
<s> "Now, this is talking" </s>
<s> cried Sharkey, jumping off the gun and holding out his hand </s>
<s> "I have not met many who could look John Sharkey in the eyes and speak with a full breath </s>
<s> May the devil seize me if I do not choose you as a consort </s>
<s> But if you play me false, then I will come aboard of you and gut you upon your own poop" </s>
<s> "And I pledge you the same" </s>
<s> said Copley Banks, and so the two pirates became sworn comrades to each other </s>
<s> That summer they went north as far as the Newfoundland Banks, and harried the New York traders and the whale-ships from New England </s>
<s> It was Copley Banks who captured the Liverpool ship, _House of Hanover_, but it was Sharkey who fastened her master to the windlass and pelted him to death with empty claret-bottles </s>
<s> Together they engaged the King's ship _Royal Fortune_, which had been sent in search of them, and beat her off after a night action of five hours, the drunken, raving crews fighting naked in the light of the battle-lanterns, with a bucket of rum and a pannikin laid by the tackles of every gun </s>
<s> They ran to Topsail Inlet in North Carolina to refit, and then in the spring they were at the Grand Caicos, ready for a long cruise down the West Indies </s>
<s> By this time Sharkey and Copley Banks had become very excellent friends, for Sharkey loved a wholehearted villain, and he loved a man of metal, and it seemed to him that the two met in the captain of the _Ruffling Harry_ </s>
<s> It was long before he gave his confidence to him, for cold suspicion lay deep in his character </s>
<s> Never once would he trust himself outside his own ship and away from his own men </s>
<s> But Copley Banks came often on board the _Happy Delivery_, and joined Sharkey in many of his morose debauches, so that at last any lingering misgivings of the latter were set at rest </s>
<s> He knew nothing of the evil that he had done to his new boon companion, for of his many victims how could he remember the woman and the two boys whom he had slain with such levity so long ago </s>
<s> When, therefore, he received a challenge to himself and to his quartermaster for a carouse upon the last evening of their stay at the Caicos Bank, he saw no reason to refuse </s>
<s> A well-found passenger ship had been rifled the week before, so their fare was of the best, and after supper five of them drank deeply together </s>
<s> There were the two captains, Birthmark Sweetlocks, Ned Galloway, and Israel Martin, the old buccaneersman </s>
<s> To wait upon them was the dumb steward, whose head Sharkey split with his glass, because he had been too slow in the filling of it </s>
<s> The quartermaster had slipped Sharkey's pistols away from him, for it was an old joke with him to fire them cross-handed under the table, and see who was the luckiest man </s>
<s> It was a pleasantry which had cost his boatswain his leg, so now, when the table was cleared, they would coax Sharkey's weapons away from him on the excuse of the heat, and lay them out of his reach </s>
<s> The Captain's cabin of the _Ruffling Harry_ was in a deck-house upon the poop, and a sternchaser gun was mounted at the back of it </s>
<s> Round shot were racked round the wall, and three great hogsheads of powder made a stand for dishes and for bottles </s>
<s> In this grim room the five pirates sang and roared and drank, while the silent steward still filled up their glasses, and passed the box and the candle round for their tobacco-pipes </s>
<s> Hour after hour the talk became fouler, the voices hoarser, the curses and shoutings more incoherent, until three of the five had closed their blood-shot eyes, and dropped their swimming heads upon the table </s>
<s> Copley Banks and Sharkey were left face to face, the one because he had drunk the least, the other because no amount of liquor would ever shake his iron nerve or warm his sluggish blood </s>
<s> Behind him stood the watchful steward, for ever filling up his waning glass </s>
<s> From without came the low lapping of the tide, and from over the water a sailor's chanty from the barque </s>
<s> In the windless tropical night the words came clearly to their ears: "A trader sailed from Stepney Town, Wake her up </s>
<s> Shake her up </s>
<s> Try her with the mainsail </s>
<s> A trader sailed from Stepney Town With a keg full of gold and a velvet gown </s>

<s> "To reach you I have had to sink to your level </s>

<s> I've robbed and I have murdered--worse still, I have laughed and lived with you--and all for the one end </s>

<s> Shake her up </s>

<s> To the dying pirate the jovial words and rollicking tune made his own fate seem the harsher, but there was no softening in his venomous blue eyes </s>

<s> He lit the candle-end as he spoke, and blew out the other lights upon the table </s>

<s> There was a skiff alongside, and in it Copley Banks and the dumb steward made their way to the beach, and looked back upon the brig riding in the moonlight just outside the shadow of the palm trees </s>

<s> And then at last there came the dull thud of a gun, and an instant later the shattering crash of the explosion </s>
<s> The long, sleek, black barque, the sweep of white sand, and the fringe of nodding, feathery palm trees sprang into dazzling light and back into darkness again </s>
<s> Voices screamed and called upon the bay </s>
<s> Then Copley Banks, his heart singing within him touched his companion upon the shoulder, and they plunged together into the lonely jungle of the Caicos </s>
<s> V THE "SLAPPING SAL" It was in the days when France's power was already broken upon the seas, and when more of her three-deckers lay rotting in the Medway than were to be found in Brest harbour </s>
<s> But her frigates and corvettes still scoured the ocean, closely followed ever by those of her rival </s>
<s> At the uttermost ends of the earth these dainty vessels, with sweet names of girls or of flowers, mangled and shattered each other for the honour of the four yards of bunting which flapped from the end of their gaffs </s>
<s> It had blown hard in the night, but the wind had dropped with the dawning, and now the rising sun tinted the fringe of the storm-wrack as it dwindled into the west and glinted on the endless crests of the long, green waves </s>
<s> To north and south and west lay a skyline which was unbroken save by the spout of foam when two of the great Atlantic seas dashed each other into spray </s>
<s> To the east was a rocky island, jutting out into craggy points, with a few scattered clumps of palm trees and a pennant of mist streaming out from the bare, conical hill which capped it </s>
<s> A heavy surf beat upon the shore, and, at a safe distance from it, the British 32-gun frigate _Leda_, Captain A </s>
<s> P </s>
<s> Johnson, raised her black, glistening side upon the crest of a wave, or swooped down into an emerald valley, dipping away to the nor'ard under easy sail </s>
<s> On her snow-white quarter-deck stood a stiff little brown-faced man, who swept the horizon with his glass </s>
<s> "Mr Wharton" </s>
<s> he cried, with a voice like a rusty hinge </s>
<s> A thin, knock-kneed officer shambled across the poop to him </s>
<s> "Yes, sir" </s>
<s> "I've opened the sealed orders, Mr Wharton" </s>
<s> A glimmer of curiosity shone upon the meagre features of the first lieutenant </s>
<s> The _Leda_ had sailed with her consort, the _Dido_, from Antigua the week before, and the admiral's orders had been contained in a sealed envelope </s>
<s> "We were to open them on reaching the deserted island of Sombriero, lying in north latitude eighteen, thirty-six, west longitude sixty-three, twenty-eight </s>
<s> Sombriero bore four miles to the north-east from our port-bow when the gale cleared, Mr Wharton" </s>

<s> TALES OF BLUE WATER VII THE STRIPED CHEST "What do you make of her, Allardyce" </s>
<s> I asked </s>
<s> My second mate was standing beside me upon the poop, with his short, thick legs astretch, for the gale had left a considerable swell behind it, and our two quarter-boats nearly touched the water with every roll </s>
<s> He steadied his glass against the mizzen-shrouds, and he looked long and hard at this disconsolate stranger every time she came reeling up on to the crest of a roller and hung balanced for a few seconds before swooping down upon the other side </s>
<s> She lay so low in the water that I could only catch an occasional glimpse of a pea-green line of bulwark </s>
<s> She was a brig, but her mainmast had been snapped short off some ten feet above the deck, and no effort seemed to have been made to cut away the wreckage, which floated, sails and yards, like the broken wing of a wounded gull, upon the water beside her </s>
<s> The foremast was still standing, but the fore-topsail was flying loose, and the head-sails were streaming out in long white pennons in front of her </s>
<s> Never have I seen a vessel which appeared to have gone through rougher handling </s>
<s> But we could not be surprised at that, for there had been times during the last three days when it was a question whether our own barque would ever see land again </s>
<s> For thirty-six hours we had kept her nose to it, and if the _Mary Sinclair_ had not been as good a seaboat as ever left the Clyde, we could not have gone through </s>
<s> And yet here we were at the end of it with the loss only of our gig and of part of the starboard bulwark </s>
<s> It did not astonish us, however, when the smother had cleared away, to find that others had been less lucky, and that this mutilated brig, staggering about upon a blue sea, and under a cloudless sky, had been left, like a blinded man after a lightning flash, to tell of the terror which is past </s>

<s> VIII THE CAPTAIN OF THE "POLESTAR" (BEING AN EXTRACT FROM THE SINGULAR JOURNAL OF JOHN M'ALISTER RAY, STUDENT OF MEDICINE.) _September 11th._--Lat </s>
<s> 81 40' N.; long </s>
<s> 2 E </s>
<s> Still lying-to amid enormous ice fields </s>
<s> The one which stretches away to the north of us, and to which our ice-anchor is attached, cannot be smaller than an English county </s>
<s> To the right and left unbroken sheets extend to the horizon </s>
<s> This morning the mate reported that there were signs of pack ice to the southward </s>
<s> Should this form of sufficient thickness to bar our return, we shall be in a position of danger, as the food, I hear, is already running somewhat short </s>
<s> It is late in the season, and the nights are beginning to reappear </s>
<s> This morning I saw a star twinkling just over the fore-yard, the first since the beginning of May </s>
<s> There is considerable discontent among the crew, many of whom are anxious to get back home to be in time for the herring season, when labour always commands a high price upon the Scotch coast </s>
<s> As yet their displeasure is only signified by sullen countenances and black looks, but I heard from the second mate this afternoon that they contemplated sending a deputation to the Captain to explain their grievance </s>
<s> I much doubt how he will receive it, as he is a man of fierce temper, and very sensitive about anything approaching to an infringement of his rights </s>
<s> I shall venture after dinner to say a few words to him upon the subject </s>
<s> I have always found that he will tolerate from me what he would resent from any other member of the crew </s>
<s> Amsterdam Island, at the north-west corner of Spitzbergen, is visible upon our starboard quarter--a rugged line of volcanic rocks, intersected by white seams, which represent glaciers </s>
<s> It is curious to think that at the present moment there is probably no human being nearer to us than the Danish settlements in the south of Greenland--a good nine hundred miles as the crow flies </s>
<s> A captain takes a great responsibility upon himself when he risks his vessel under such circumstances </s>
<s> No whaler has ever remained in these latitudes till so advanced a period of the year </s>
<s> 9 P.M.--I have spoken to Captain Craigie, and though the result has been hardly satisfactory, I am bound to say that he listened to what I had to say very quietly and even deferentially </s>
<s> When I had finished he put on that air of iron determination which I have frequently observed upon his face, and paced rapidly backwards and forwards across the narrow cabin for some minutes </s>
<s> At first I feared that I had seriously offended him, but he dispelled the idea by sitting down again, and putting his hand upon my arm with a gesture which almost amounted to a caress </s>
<s> There was a depth of tenderness too in his wild dark eyes which surprised me considerably </s>
<s> "Look here, Doctor," he said, "I'm sorry I ever took you--I am indeed--and I would give fifty pounds this minute to see you standing safe upon the Dundee quay </s>

<s> It is the first time that he has ever shown me anything but courtesy and kindness </s>
<s> I can hear him pacing excitedly up and down overhead as I write these lines </s>
<s> I should like to give a sketch of the character of this man, but it seems presumptuous to attempt such a thing upon paper, when the idea in my own mind is at best a vague and uncertain one </s>
<s> Several times I have thought that I grasped the clue which might explain it, but only to be disappointed by his presenting himself in some new light which would upset all my conclusions </s>
<s> It may be that no human eye but my own shall ever rest upon these lines, yet as a psychological study I shall attempt to leave some record of Captain Nicholas Craigie </s>
<s> A man's outer case generally gives some indication of the soul within </s>
<s> The Captain is tall and well-formed, with dark, handsome face, and a curious way of twitching his limbs, which may arise from nervousness, or be simply an outcome of his excessive energy </s>
<s> His jaw and whole cast of countenance is manly and resolute, but the eyes are the distinctive feature of his face </s>
<s> They are of the very darkest hazel, bright and eager, with a singular mixture of recklessness in their expression, and of something else which I have sometimes thought was more allied with horror than any other emotion </s>

<s> He sleeps badly, and I have heard him shouting during the night, but his cabin is some little distance from mine, and I could never distinguish the words which he said </s>
<s> This is one phase of his character, and the most disagreeable one </s>
<s> It is only through my close association with him, thrown together as we are day after day, that I have observed it </s>
<s> Otherwise he is an agreeable companion, well-read and entertaining, and as gallant a seaman as ever trod a deck </s>

<s> _September 12th._--Calm, clear day, and still lying in the same position </s>
<s> What wind there is comes from the south-east, but it is very slight </s>
<s> Captain is in a better humour, and apologised to me at breakfast for his rudeness </s>
<s> He still looks somewhat distrait, however, and retains that wild look in his eyes which in a Highlander would mean that he was "fey"--at least so our chief engineer remarked to me, and he has some reputation among the Celtic portion of our crew as a seer and expounder of omens </s>
<s> It is strange that superstition should have obtained such mastery over this hard-headed and practical race </s>
<s> I could not have believed to what an extent it is carried had I not observed it for myself </s>
<s> We have had a perfect epidemic of it this voyage, until I have felt inclined to serve out rations of sedatives and nerve-tonics with the Saturday allowance of grog </s>
<s> The first symptom of it was that shortly after leaving Shetland the men at the wheel used to complain that they heard plaintive cries and screams in the wake of the ship, as if something were following it and were unable to overtake it </s>
<s> This fiction has been kept up during the whole voyage, and on dark nights at the beginning of the seal-fishing it was only with great difficulty that men could be induced to do their spell </s>
<s> No doubt what they heard was either the creaking of the rudder-chains, or the cry of some passing sea-bird </s>

<s> The men, however, are so absurdly positive upon the subject that it is hopeless to argue with them </s>
<s> I mentioned the matter to the Captain once, but to my surprise he took it very gravely, and indeed appeared to be considerably disturbed by what I told him </s>
<s> I should have thought that he at least would have been above such vulgar delusions </s>

<s> It is quite refreshing to have some new topic of conversation after the eternal routine of bears and whales which has served us for so many months </s>

<s> "I was on the bridge," he said, "about four bells in the middle watch, just when the night was at its darkest </s>
<s> There was a bit of a moon, but the clouds were blowing across it so that you couldn't see far from the ship </s>

<s> I've been seventeen years to the country and I never heard seal, old or young, make a sound like that </s>

<s> I fancy what he saw must, in spite of his denial, have been a young bear erect upon its hind legs, an attitude which they often assume when alarmed </s>
<s> In the uncertain light this would bear a resemblance to a human figure, especially to a man whose nerves were already somewhat shaken </s>

<s> Their looks are more sullen than before, and their discontent more open </s>

<s> Apart from this absurd outbreak of superstition, things are looking rather more cheerful </s>

<s> _September 13th._--Had an interesting conversation with the chief mate, Mr Milne, upon the bridge </s>
<s> It seems that our captain is as great an enigma to the seamen, and even to the owners of the vessel, as he has been to me </s>
<s> Mr Milne tells me that when the ship is paid off, upon returning from a voyage, Captain Craigie disappears, and is not seen again until the approach of another season, when he walks quietly into the office of the company, and asks whether his services will be required </s>
<s> He has no friend in Dundee, nor does any one pretend to be acquainted with his early history </s>
<s> His position depends entirely upon his skill as a seaman, and the name for courage and coolness which he had earned in the capacity of mate, before being entrusted with a separate command </s>
<s> The unanimous opinion seems to be that he is not a Scotchman, and that his name is an assumed one </s>

<s> It was certainly a strange coincidence </s>
<s> The wind is veering round in an easterly direction, but is still very slight </s>
<s> I think the ice is lying closer than it did yesterday </s>
<s> As far as the eye can reach on every side there is one wide expanse of spotless white, only broken by an occasional rift or the dark shadow of a hummock </s>

<s> The Captain is taking a heavy responsibility upon himself </s>

<s> 7.30 P.M.--My deliberate opinion is that we are commanded by a madman </s>
<s> Nothing else can account for the extraordinary vagaries of Captain Craigie </s>

<s> Situated as we are on the edge of the main Arctic pack, or the "barrier" as it is called by the whalers, any wind from the north has the effect of shredding out the ice around us and allowing our escape, while a wind from the south blows up all the loose ice behind us and hems us in between two packs </s>
<s> God help us, I say again </s>
<s> _September 14th._--Sunday, and a day of rest </s>
<s> My fears have been confirmed, and the thin strip of blue water has disappeared from the southward </s>
<s> Nothing but the great motionless ice fields around us, with their weird hummocks and fantastic pinnacles </s>
<s> There is a deathly silence over their wide expanse which is horrible </s>
<s> No lapping of the waves now, no cries of seagulls or straining of sails, but one deep universal silence in which the murmurs of the seamen, and the creak of their boots upon the white shining deck, seem discordant and out of place </s>
<s> Our only visitor was an Arctic fox, a rare animal upon the pack, though common enough upon the land </s>
<s> He did not come near the ship, however, but after surveying us from a distance fled rapidly across the ice </s>
<s> This was curious conduct, as they generally know nothing of man, and being of an inquisitive nature, become so familiar that they are easily captured </s>
<s> Incredible as it may seem, even this little incident produced a bad effect upon the crew </s>

<s> The Captain remained in seclusion all day except for about half an hour in the afternoon, when he came out upon the quarter-deck </s>

<s> Divine service was read as usual by the chief engineer </s>
<s> It is a curious thing that in whaling vessels the Church of England Prayer-book is always employed, although there is never a member of that Church among either officers or crew </s>
<s> Our men are all Roman Catholics or Presbyterians, the former predominating </s>
<s> Since a ritual is used which is foreign to both, neither can complain that the other is preferred to them, and they listen with all attention and devotion, so that the system has something to recommend it </s>

<s> _September 15th._--To-day is Flora's birthday </s>
<s> Dear lass </s>
<s> it is well that she cannot see her boy, as she used to call me, shut up among the ice fields with a crazy captain and a few weeks' provisions </s>

<s> There is but little wind, and what there is comes from an unfavourable quarter </s>

<s> His former unpopularity was forgotten, and the old harpooner whom I have already mentioned for his superstition, led off three cheers, which were heartily joined in by all hands </s>
<s> _September 16th._--The wind has veered round to the north during the night, and the ice shows some symptoms of opening out </s>
<s> The men are in good humour in spite of the short allowance upon which they have been placed </s>
<s> Steam is kept up in the engine-room, that there may be no delay should an opportunity for escape present itself </s>
<s> The Captain is in exuberant spirits, though he still retains that wild "fey" expression which I have already remarked upon </s>
<s> This burst of cheerfulness puzzles me more than his former gloom </s>
<s> I cannot understand it </s>
<s> I think I mentioned in an early part of this journal that one of his oddities is that he never permits any person to enter his cabin, but insists upon making his own bed, such as it is, and performing every other office for himself </s>

<s> Were he a less reserved man I should make some remark upon the subject </s>

<s> 11.20 P.M.--Captain just gone to bed after a long and interesting conversation on general topics </s>

<s> The wind is freshening up, and blows steadily from the north </s>
<s> The nights are as dark now as they are in England </s>
<s> I hope to-morrow may set us free from our frozen fetters </s>
<s> _September 17th._--The Bogie again </s>
<s> Thank Heaven that I have strong nerves </s>
<s> The superstition of these poor fellows, and the circumstantial accounts which they give, with the utmost earnestness and self-conviction, would horrify any man not accustomed to their ways </s>
<s> There are many versions of the matter, but the sum-total of them all is that something uncanny has been flitting round the ship all night, and that Sandie M'Donald of Peterhead and "lang" Peter Williamson of Shetland saw it, as also did Mr Milne on the bridge--so, having three witnesses, they can make a better case of it than the second mate did </s>

<s> Ye would na' be sae ready to put it a' doon to auld wives' clavers then, I'm thinkin'" </s>

<s> Should the wind continue favourable it will break up as rapidly as it formed </s>
<s> At present we can do nothing but smoke and wait and hope for the best </s>
<s> I am rapidly becoming a fatalist </s>
<s> When dealing with such uncertain factors as wind and ice a man can be nothing else </s>

<s> These spectral alarms have a very bad effect upon the Captain </s>

<s> The night was very dark--so dark that, standing under the quarter-boat, I was unable to see the officer upon the bridge </s>
<s> I think I have already mentioned the extraordinary silence which prevails in these frozen seas </s>
<s> In other parts of the world, be they ever so barren, there is some slight vibration of the air--some faint hum, be it from the distant haunts of men, or from the leaves of the trees, of the wings of the birds, or even the faint rustle of the grass that covers the ground </s>

<s> * * * * * The long-impending catastrophe has come at last </s>
<s> I hardly know what to write about it </s>
<s> The Captain is gone </s>
<s> He may come back to us again alive, but I fear me--I fear me </s>
<s> It is now seven o'clock of the morning of the 19th of September </s>
<s> I have spent the whole night traversing the great ice-floe in front of us with a party of seamen in the hope of coming upon some trace of him, but in vain </s>
<s> I shall try to give some account of the circumstances which attended upon his disappearance </s>

<s> My inferences are my own, but I shall be answerable for the facts </s>

<s> 7.30 P.M.--Just returned dead beat and utterly tired out from a second unsuccessful search for the Captain </s>
<s> The floe is of enormous extent, for though we have traversed at least twenty miles of its surface, there has been no sign of its coming to an end </s>
<s> The frost has been so severe of late that the overlying snow is frozen as hard as granite, otherwise we might have had the foot-steps to guide us </s>
<s> The crew are anxious that we should cast off and steam round the floe and so to the southward, for the ice has opened up during the night, and the sea is visible upon the horizon </s>
<s> They argue that Captain Craigie is certainly dead, and that we are all risking our lives to no purpose by remaining when we have an opportunity of escape </s>
<s> Mr Milne and I have had the greatest difficulty in persuading them to wait until to-morrow night, and have been compelled to promise that we will not under any circumstances delay our departure longer than that </s>
<s> We propose therefore to take a few hours' sleep, and then to start upon a final search </s>
<s> _September 20th, evening._--I crossed the ice this morning with a party of men exploring the southern part of the floe, while Mr Milne went off in a northerly direction </s>
<s> We pushed on for ten or twelve miles without seeing a trace of any living thing except a single bird, which fluttered a great way over our heads, and which by its flight I should judge to have been a falcon </s>
<s> The southern extremity of the ice field tapered away into a long narrow spit which projected out into the sea </s>

<s> We had hardly gone a hundred yards before M'Donald of Peterhead cried out that he saw something in front of us, and began to run </s>
<s> We all got a glimpse of it and ran too </s>
<s> At first it was only a vague darkness against the white ice, but as we raced along together it took the shape of a man, and eventually of the man of whom we were in search </s>
<s> He was lying face downwards upon a frozen bank </s>
<s> Many little crystals of ice and feathers of snow had drifted on to him as he lay, and sparkled upon his dark seaman's jacket </s>

<s> I have learned never to ridicule any man's opinion, however strange it may seem </s>
<s> Sure it is that Captain Nicholas Craigie had met with no painful end, for there was a bright smile upon his blue pinched features, and his hands were still outstretched as though grasping at the strange visitor which had summoned him away into the dim world that lies beyond the grave </s>

<s> There he shall lie, with his secret and his sorrows and his mystery all still buried in his breast, until that great day when the sea shall give up its dead, and Nicholas Craigie come out from among the ice with the smile upon his face, and his stiffened arms outstretched in greeting </s>

<s> * * * * * Note by Dr </s>
<s> John M'Alister Ray, senior.--I have read over the strange events connected with the death of the Captain of the _Polestar_, as narrated in the journal of my son </s>
<s> That everything occurred exactly as he describes it I have the fullest confidence, and, indeed, the most positive certainty, for I know him to be a strong-nerved and unimaginative man, with the strictest regard for veracity </s>
<s> Still, the story is, on the face of it, so vague and so improbable, that I was long opposed to its publication </s>
<s> Within the last few days, however, I have had independent testimony upon the subject which throws a new light upon it </s>
<s> I had run down to Edinburgh to attend a meeting of the British Medical Association, when I chanced to come across Dr </s>
<s> P.----, an old college chum of mine, now practising at Saltash, in Devonshire </s>
<s> Upon my telling him of this experience of my son's, he declared to me that he was familiar with the man, and proceeded, to my no small surprise, to give me a description of him, which tallied remarkably well with that given in the journal, except that he depicted him as a younger man </s>
<s> According to his account, he had been engaged to a young lady of singular beauty residing upon the Cornish coast </s>
<s> During his absence at sea his betrothed had died under circumstances of peculiar horror </s>
<s> IX THE FIEND OF THE COOPERAGE It was no easy matter to bring the _Gamecock_ up to the island, for the river had swept down so much silt that the banks extended for many miles out into the Atlantic </s>
<s> The coast was hardly to be seen when the first white curl of the breakers warned us of our danger, and from there onwards we made our way very carefully under mainsail and jib, keeping the broken water well to the left, as is indicated on the chart </s>
<s> More than once her bottom touched the sand (we were drawing something under six feet at the time), but we had always way enough and luck enough to carry us through </s>
<s> Finally, the water shoaled, very rapidly, but they had sent a canoe from the factory, and the Krooboy pilot brought us within two hundred yards of the island </s>
<s> Here we dropped our anchor, for the gestures of the negro indicated that we could not hope to get any farther </s>
<s> The blue of the sea had changed to the brown of the river, and, even under the shelter of the island, the current was singing and swirling round our bows </s>
<s> The stream appeared to be in spate, for it was over the roots of the palm trees, and everywhere upon its muddy, greasy surface we could see logs of wood and debris of all sorts which had been carried down by the flood </s>
<s> When I had assured myself that we swung securely at our moorings, I thought it best to begin watering at once, for the place looked as if it reeked with fever </s>
<s> The heavy river, the muddy, shining banks, the bright poisonous green of the jungle, the moist steam in the air, they were all so many danger signals to one who could read them </s>
<s> I sent the long-boat off, therefore, with two large hogsheads, which should be sufficient to last us until we made St </s>
<s> Paul de Loanda </s>
<s> For my own part I took the dinghy and rowed for the island, for I could see the Union Jack fluttering above the palms to mark the position of Armitage and Wilson's trading station </s>
<s> When I had cleared the grove, I could see the place, a long, low, whitewashed building, with a deep verandah in front, and an immense pile of palm oil barrels heaped upon either flank of it </s>
<s> A row of surf boats and canoes lay along the beach, and a single small jetty projected into the river </s>
<s> Two men in white suits with red cummerbunds round their waists were waiting upon the end of it to receive me </s>
<s> One was a large portly fellow with a greyish beard </s>
<s> The other was slender and tall, with a pale pinched face, which was half concealed by a great mushroom-shaped hat </s>
<s> "Very glad to see you," said the latter, cordially </s>
<s> "I am Walker, the agent of Armitage and Wilson </s>

<s> Severall of the same company </s>

<s> "I'm owner and captain--Meldrum is the name" </s>
<s> "Exploring" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> "I'm a lepidopterist--a butterfly-catcher </s>
<s> I've been doing the west coast from Senegal downwards" </s>
<s> "Good sport" </s>
<s> asked the Doctor, turning a slow yellow-shot eye upon me </s>
<s> "I have forty cases full </s>
<s> We came in here to water, and also to see what you have in my line" </s>

<s> "What do we do" </s>
<s> said the Doctor, when I had begun asking questions in my turn </s>
<s> "Our business keeps us pretty busy, and in our leisure time we talk politics" </s>
<s> "Yes, by the special mercy of Providence Severall is a rank Radical, and I am a good stiff Unionist, and we talk Home Rule for two solid hours every evening" </s>

<s> X JELLAND'S VOYAGE "Well," said our Anglo-Jap as we all drew up our chairs round the smoking-room fire, "it's an old tale out yonder, and may have spilt over into print for all I know </s>
<s> I don't want to turn this club-room into a chestnut stall, but it is a long way to the Yellow Sea, and it is just as likely that none of you have ever heard of the yawl _Matilda_, and of what happened to Henry Jelland and Willy McEvoy aboard of her </s>
<s> "The middle of the sixties was a stirring time out in Japan </s>
<s> That was just after the Simonosaki bombardment, and before the Daimio affair </s>
<s> There was a Tory party and there was a Liberal party among the natives, and the question that they were wrangling over was whether the throats of the foreigners should be cut or not </s>
<s> I tell you all, politics have been tame to me since then </s>
<s> If you lived in a treaty port, you were bound to wake up and take an interest in them </s>
<s> And to make it better, the outsider had no way of knowing how the game was going </s>
<s> If the opposition won it would not be a newspaper paragraph that would tell him of it, but a good old Tory in a suit of chain mail, with a sword in each hand, would drop in and let him know all about it in a single upper cut </s>
<s> "Of course it makes men reckless when they are living on the edge of a volcano like that </s>
<s> Just at first they are very jumpy, and then there comes a time when they learn to enjoy life while they have it </s>
<s> I tell you there's nothing makes life so beautiful as when the shadow of death begins to fall across it </s>
<s> Time is too precious to be dawdled away then, and a man lives every minute of it </s>
<s> That was the way with us in Yokohama </s>
<s> There were many European places of business which had to go on running, and the men who worked them made the place lively for seven nights in the week </s>
<s> "One of the heads of the European colony was Randolph Moore, the big export merchant </s>
<s> His offices were in Yokohama, but he spent a good deal of his time at his house up in Jeddo, which had only just been opened to the trade </s>
<s> In his absence he used to leave his affairs in the hands of his head clerk, Jelland, whom he knew to be a man of great energy and resolution </s>
<s> But energy and resolution are two-edged things, you know, and when they are used against you you don't appreciate them so much </s>
<s> "It was gambling that set Jelland wrong </s>
